### [1] [WIP: Software Engineering Competencies in the Age of AI](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12259v1)
*Lynn Vonderhaar,Massood Towhidnejad,Omar Ochoa*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文基于行业AI需求文献，提出在软件工程胜任力模型中增加AI素养和AI开发两个新胜任力，并分析了所需技能领域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有胜任力模型未能及时反映行业对AI技能的快速变化需求，需要补充AI相关胜任力。

Method: 通过文献回顾分析行业AI需求，提出新的胜任力，并基于需求推导技能领域。

Result: 提出了AI素养和AI开发两个新胜任力，并明确了各自所需的技能领域。

Conclusion: 应将AI素养和AI开发纳入SWECOM，以更好地匹配行业需求。

中文摘要：大学教育的目的是让毕业生充分准备好进入并在其领域中成功就业。认证机构和专业组织通过发布课程内容、技能和胜任力模型，来概述大学在学位项目中必须教授的基础知识，从而帮助实现这一目标。尽管这些课程指南和胜任力模型会定期更新，以使大学课程与当前行业需求保持一致，但行业需求迅速演变，往往无法在模型中得到适当反映，这种情况目前正随着人工智能在行业中的兴起而出现。本文回顾了描述行业内AI需求的文献，以激励在软件工程胜任力模型（SWECOM）中增加两个新的AI胜任力：AI素养和AI开发。然后，本文分析了文献中描述的行业需求，以提出这些新胜任力所需的技能领域。

Original abstract: A university education is meant to fully prepare graduates to enter and succeed in the workforce in their field. Accreditation bodies and professional organizations help to achieve this by publishing curriculum content, skills and competency models to outline the basics that universities must teach within a degree program. Although these curriculum guidelines and competency models are periodically updated to align university curricula with current industry needs, the needs of industry evolve rapidly and are often not properly reflected within the model, a situation which is occurring now with the rise of Artificial Intelligence (AI) use in industry. This paper reviews literature describing the AI needs within industry to motivate two new AI competencies, AI Literacy and AI development, within the Software Engineering Competency Model (SWECOM). This work then analyzes the industry needs described in the literature to propose the necessary skill areas for these new competencies.

</details>


### [2] [Code-MUE: Measuring Code LLMs' Uncertainty through Execution-based Semantic Interaction Graphs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12273v1)
*Xiaoning Ren,Yinxing Xue,Lei Ma,Yuheng Huang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出了Code-MUE，一个黑盒不确定性估计框架，通过基于执行的语义交互图和冯·诺依曼熵来度量代码生成的不确定性，在八个LLM上实现了与功能正确性高达-0.98的斯皮尔曼相关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的不确定性估计方法不适用于闭源模型，且标准文本指标无法捕捉代码语义与语法之间的差异，导致无法有效区分可靠预测与随机猜测。

Method: Code-MUE使用纯黑盒方法，通过执行代码生成语义交互图，并计算解空间的冯·诺依曼熵来量化语义多样性，从而估计不确定性。

Result: 在八个最先进的LLM上，Code-MUE与功能正确性达到强负相关（斯皮尔曼相关系数高达-0.98），显著优于词汇和嵌入基线方法。

Conclusion: Code-MUE能够有效进行代码生成的不确定性估计，支持风险检测和选择性预测，提升自动化可靠性。

中文摘要：随着代码大型语言模型（LLM）成为现代软件工程的核心，其固有的随机性带来了显著的实际风险，即使是微小的错误也可能导致严重的功能、安全或可靠性后果。因此，可靠的自动化需要具备区分有信心的、有充分支持的预测与随机猜测的能力。然而，现有的不确定性估计方法面临一个关键空白：白盒和灰盒技术通常不适用于闭源模型，而标准的“黑盒”文本指标无法捕捉代码特有的脆弱性，因为语法变化并不总是意味着语义分歧。为了弥合这一语法-语义差距，我们引入了Code-MUE，这是一个纯粹的黑盒框架，通过基于执行的语义交互图来测量不确定性。与依赖表面文本相似性的先前方法不同，Code-MUE将不确定性建立在可观察的运行时行为上，计算解空间的冯·诺依曼熵以量化全局语义多样性。一项涵盖八个最先进LLM的大规模实证研究表明，Code-MUE与功能正确性实现了强负相关（斯皮尔曼相关系数高达-0.98），显著优于基于词汇和嵌入的基线方法，同时在实际工作流程中实现了稳健的风险检测和选择性预测。

Original abstract: As Code Large Language Models (LLMs) become central to modern software engineering, their inherent stochasticity poses significant real-world risks, where even minor errors can lead to severe functional, security, or safety consequences. Reliable automation, therefore, demands the ability to distinguish between confident, well-supported predictions and stochastic guessing. However, existing uncertainty estimation methods face a critical gap: white and grey-box techniques are often inapplicable to closed-source models, while standard "black-box" text metrics fail to capture the unique fragility of code, where syntactic variation does not always imply semantic divergence. To bridge this syntax-semantics gap, we introduce Code-MUE, a purely black-box framework that measures uncertainty through execution-based Semantic Interaction Graphs. Unlike prior approaches that rely on superficial textual similarity, Code-MUE grounds uncertainty in observable runtime behavior, calculating the Von Neumann entropy of the solution space to quantify global semantic diversity. A large-scale empirical study across eight state-of-the-art LLMs demonstrates that Code-MUE achieves a strong negative correlation with functional correctness (Spearman's correlation up to -0.98), significantly outperforming lexical and embedding-based baselines while enabling robust risk detection and selective prediction in practical workflows.

</details>


### [3] [XScientist: A Git-Like Research Protocol for Long-Running Autonomous Scientific Discovery](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12301v1)
*Jixiang Luo*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: XScientist是一个类似git的研究协议和操作系统，通过将每次运行视为可移植的研究产物（ARA）而非仅PDF，解决了自主研究系统难以信任的操作问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的自主研究系统通常被视为一次性论文生成器，忽略了研究长期运行、分支、易失败且依赖可审计交接的操作问题，导致难以信任。

Method: XScientist设计了一个git-like的协议和操作系统，包括想法生成、实验执行、手稿起草、自我审查、修复、质量门控、守护进程调度等，并导出Agent-Native Research Artifact (ARA)协议，记录探索DAG、代码、输出、声明-证据锚点、内容哈希、溯源和重新执行钩子。

Result: 系统能够生成可检查的科学探索树，包含失败分支、修复实验、消融和手稿声明，并支持确定性完整性取证、样本门控、真相合约、评审者修复循环和守护进程控制。

Conclusion: XScientist提供了将自主科学从单次运行演示转向可重现、可评审和可分支的研究基础设施的实际保障措施，其实现和手稿在GitHub上公开维护。

中文摘要：自主研究系统通常被评估为一次性论文生成器：给定一个主题，它们会生成手稿和一小部分实验日志。这种框架隐藏了使此类系统难以信任的操作问题：研究是长期运行、分支、易失败且依赖于代理和人类之间可审计交接的。XScientist是一个类似git的研究协议和操作系统，适用于这种场景。它协调想法生成、实验执行、手稿起草、自我审查、修复、质量门控、守护进程调度和可重复性产物，形成一个持续可观测的流水线。核心设计选择是将每次运行视为一个可移植的研究产物，而不仅仅是一个PDF。XScientist导出了一个代理原生研究产物（ARA），这是一个记录探索DAG、每节点代码和输出、声明到证据锚点、内容哈希、溯源和重新执行钩子的协议。这使得每篇生成的论文都可以作为科学探索树进行检查：失败的分支、修复的实验、消融和手稿声明仍然与生成它们的节点相连。该系统还包括确定性完整性取证、样本门控、真相合约、评审者导向的修复循环和长期运行的守护进程控制。本文描述了当前XScientist的架构、ARA协议表面以及将自主科学从单次运行演示推向可重现、可评审和可分支的研究基础设施所需的实际保障措施。实现和手稿源代码维护在公开的GitHub仓库https://github.com/smileformylove/XScientist中。

Original abstract: Autonomous research systems are often evaluated as one-shot paper generators: given a topic, they produce a manuscript and a small set of experiment logs. This framing hides the operational problem that makes such systems difficult to trust: research is long-running, branching, failure-prone, and dependent on auditable handoffs between agents and humans. XScientist is a git-like research protocol and operating system for this setting. It orchestrates idea generation, experiment execution, manuscript drafting, self-review, repair, quality gating, daemon scheduling, and reproducibility artifacts as one continuously observable pipeline. The central design choice is to treat each run as a portable research artifact rather than only as a PDF. XScientist exports an Agent-Native Research Artifact (ARA), a protocol that records an exploration DAG, per-node code and outputs, claim-to-evidence anchors, content hashes, provenance, and re-execution hooks. This makes each generated paper inspectable as a science exploration tree: failed branches, repaired experiments, ablations, and manuscript claims remain connected to the nodes that produced them. The system also includes deterministic integrity forensics, sample gates, truth contracts, reviewer-oriented repair loops, and long-running daemon controls. This paper describes the current XScientist architecture, the ARA protocol surface, and the practical safeguards needed to move autonomous science from single-run demos toward reproducible, reviewable, and forkable research infrastructure. The implementation and manuscript source are maintained in the public GitHub repository at https://github.com/smileformylove/XScientist.

</details>


### [4] [How Many Interviews Are Enough in a Software Engineering Study? Preliminary Findings on Sample Size and Saturation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12326v1)
*Ronnie de Souza Santos,Italo Santos,Mauricio Rodrigues,Cleyton Magalhaes*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过分析2016-2025年软件工程领域主要期刊会议中的访谈研究，发现样本量多在13-24之间，但饱和度与充分性报告质量不一，多依赖隐式推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 访谈样本充分性和饱和度在软件工程文献中报告不一致，缺乏系统的方法论指导。

Method: 分析了2016-2025年间主要软件工程场所的论文，关注样本量、饱和度讨论和充分性理由。

Result: 样本量差异大，常见少于12人；最频繁范围为13-24人；饱和度和充分性理由异质，多依赖隐式推理。

Conclusion: 提供了访谈研究方法报告实践的初步实证见解，促进了定性严谨性和透明度的讨论。

中文摘要：背景：基于访谈的研究在经验软件工程中被广泛用于调查人类、组织和社会技术现象，然而文献中对访谈样本充分性和饱和度的报告不一致。目的：本文研究访谈样本充分性和饱和度在经验软件工程研究中是如何被操作化的。方法：我们分析了2016年至2025年间在主要软件工程场所发表的论文，重点关注访谈样本量、饱和度讨论以及样本充分性理由。结果：初步发现表明样本量存在显著差异，从高度专业化的少量样本研究到涉及大量访谈数据的更广泛调查。少于12名受访者的研究很常见，并且通常与专业工业背景或有限的组织访问权限相关。然而，最常出现的范围是13到24名受访者，这表明中等规模的样本是经验软件工程研究中最常见的配置。饱和度和样本充分性理由存在异质性，许多研究依赖隐式或上下文推理，而非明确的方法论讨论。结论：我们的研究结果为基于访谈的软件工程研究中的方法论报告实践提供了初步的实证见解，并有助于关于定性严谨性和透明度的持续讨论。

Original abstract: Background. Interview based studies are widely used in empirical software engineering to investigate human, organizational, and socio technical phenomena, yet interview sample adequacy and saturation are reported inconsistently across the literature. Aims. This paper investigates how interview sample adequacy and saturation are operationalized in empirical software engineering research. Method. We analyzed papers published between 2016 and 2025 across major software engineering venues, focusing on interview sample sizes, saturation discussions, and sample adequacy justifications. Results. Preliminary findings indicate substantial variation in sample sizes, from highly specialized small sample studies to broader investigations involving large interview datasets. Studies involving fewer than 12 interviewees were common and frequently associated with specialized industrial contexts or constrained organizational access. However, the most recurrent range was 13 to 24 interviewees, suggesting that moderate sized samples represent the most common configuration in empirical software engineering research. Saturation and sample adequacy justification were heterogeneous, with many studies relying on implicit or contextual reasoning rather than explicit methodological discussion. Conclusions. Our findings provide initial empirical insights into methodological reporting practices in interview based software engineering research and contribute to ongoing discussions regarding qualitative rigor and transparency.

</details>


### [5] [Skills That Don't Exist: A Large-Scale Study of Hallucinated Skill Recommendation in LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12340v1)
*Weifeng Yuan,Wenbo Guo,Feng Dong,Haoyu Wang,Yang Liu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: LLM代理存在技能名称幻觉漏洞，攻击者可预注册恶意技能，测量显示幻觉率约36-37%，现有防御严重损害可用性，需生态系统级修复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 发现LLM代理在推荐技能时会凭空捏造不存在的技能名称，这可能导致供应链攻击，但此前缺乏系统性测量和防御研究。

Method: 对15,000个提示在12种配置（4个独立LLM和8个代理）下进行大规模测量，统计缺失于所有注册表和GitHub的技能名称作为幻觉，并测试4种模型级防御。

Result: 所有配置均存在幻觉，独立LLM平均36.0%，代理36.9%，真实问题达43.1%；共产生5,669个不同幻觉名称；名称重复性高；最强防御（检索接地）降低幻觉率至3.2%但可用性剧降（正确推荐仅1/6）。

Conclusion: 技能名称幻觉是高度可利用的漏洞，修复需要生态系统级结构变革，如注册表名称预留和验证推荐流水线，而非仅靠提示工程或模型调优。

中文摘要：LLM代理通过从开放注册表中下载技能来获取新能力。开发者通常不会手动浏览这些目录，而是要求代理推荐并安装一个技能。这种便利性隐藏了一个风险：代理经常发明在注册表中不存在的技能名称。我们将此缺陷称为技能名称幻觉。一个虚假的名称看似无害，但它为供应链攻击打开了大门。由于注册表很少验证发布者，攻击者可以提示代理，收集它返回的虚假名称，预先在这些名称下注册恶意技能，并等待受害者安装负载。我们首次对技能名称幻觉进行了大规模测量，评估了12种配置（4个独立LLM和8个代理）下的15,000个提示。我们保守地将名称视为幻觉，仅当它同时缺失于所有实时注册表和GitHub。结果揭示了一个系统性漏洞：每种配置都会产生幻觉。独立LLM的平均幻觉率为36.0%，代理为36.9%，在真实世界开发者问题上则上升到43.1%。总共，系统生成了5,669个不同的幻觉名称。关键的是，这些名称并非随机噪声。代理在不同提示和模型之间重复相同的虚假名称，为攻击者提供了高度可靠的目标进行劫持。最后，我们测试了四种模型级别的防御措施，发现安全性与可用性之间存在严重冲突。最强的防御——检索接地，将幻觉率从40.8%降至3.2%，但严重削弱了实用性：即使是防御最好的系统，也只有大约六分之一的情况下能推荐正确的技能。因此，技能名称幻觉是一个高度可利用的漏洞，只需最小的攻击者努力。修复它不能仅依赖提示工程或模型调优。它需要生态系统范围的结构性变革：注册表级别的名称预留和经过验证的推荐流水线。

Original abstract: LLM agents acquire new capabilities by downloading skills from open registries. Instead of browsing these catalogs manually, developers typically ask the agent to recommend and install a skill. This convenience hides a risk: agents frequently invent names for skills that exist in no registry. We term this flaw skill name hallucination. A fake name may seem harmless, but it opens the door to supply-chain attacks. Because registries rarely verify publishers, an adversary can prompt the agent, collect the fake names it returns, pre-register malicious skills under them, and wait for a victim to install the payload. We conducted the first large-scale measurement of skill name hallucination, evaluating 15,000 prompts across 12 configurations (4 standalone LLMs and 8 agents). We conservatively counted a name as hallucinated only if it was missing from all live registries and GitHub. The results reveal a systemic vulnerability: every configuration hallucinates. Rates average 36.0% for standalone LLMs and 36.9% for agents, rising to 43.1% on real-world developer questions. In total, the systems generated 5,669 distinct hallucinated names. Crucially, these names are not random noise. Agents repeat the same fake names across prompts and models, giving attackers highly reliable targets to hijack. Finally, we tested four model-level defenses and found a severe conflict between security and usability. The strongest, retrieval grounding, cut the hallucination rate from 40.8% to 3.2% but crippled usefulness: even the best-defended system recommended the correct skill only about one in six times. Skill name hallucination is thus a highly exploitable vulnerability requiring minimal attacker effort. Fixing it cannot rely on prompt engineering or model tuning alone. It demands ecosystem-wide structural changes: registry-level name reservations and verified recommendation pipelines.

</details>


### [6] [Detecting Rendering Bugs in Imperative Data Visualization Libraries via Equivalent Mutations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12363v3)
*Weiqi Lu,Yongqiang Tian*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: VIZDETOUR通过等价突变自动检测命令式数据可视化库的渲染错误，将预言问题转化为等价检查，并在三个流行库中发现47个新错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 命令式数据可视化库的渲染错误难以自动检测，因为缺乏预期渲染的预言，且微小更新可能导致视觉不一致。

Method: 通过追加语义等价的API调用序列（突变）来改变执行路径但保持最终渲染不变，然后比较原始与突变脚本的渲染输出（使用感知哈希），从而将预言问题转化为等价检查。

Result: 在matplotlib、bokeh和plotly上评估，发现47个以前未知的渲染错误，其中39个已确认，18个已修复。

Conclusion: VIZDETOUR有效检测了命令式数据可视化库中的渲染错误，将预言问题转化为等价检查是一个可行的自动化测试方法。

中文摘要：命令式数据可视化库通过一系列有状态的API调用来构建绘图，这些调用会逐步创建和更新图形元素。这些库中的渲染错误通常表现为不正确的视觉输出，而不是崩溃或异常，因此难以自动检测。一个根本性的挑战是缺乏一个能指定任意绘图脚本预期渲染的预言。此外，对一个图形元素的更新可能会无意中影响其他元素或属性，导致最终渲染图像中出现微妙的差异。本文提出了VIZDETOUR，一种通过等价突变来自动检测命令式数据可视化库中渲染错误的测试方法。关键思想是将预言问题转化为等价检查问题。从一个种子绘图脚本开始，VIZDETOUR追加一系列语义等价的API调用，这些调用会临时修改可视化状态然后将其恢复到原始状态。尽管这些突变执行了不同的执行路径，但它们应该保持最终的渲染不变。因此，原始脚本和突变脚本之间的任何视觉差异都表明存在渲染错误。为了生成这样的突变，VIZDETOUR从种子脚本构建渲染树，识别可追踪的图形元素和可变属性，并合成保持端点不变的突变序列。然后它使用感知哈希来比较渲染输出。我们在matplotlib、bokeh和plotly上使用从其官方示例库收集的脚本评估VIZDETOUR。VIZDETOUR发现了47个以前未知的错误，其中39个已确认，18个已修复。

Original abstract: Imperative data visualization libraries construct plots through a sequence of stateful API calls that incrementally create and update graphic elements. Rendering bugs in these libraries often manifest as incorrect visual outputs rather than crashes or exceptions, making them difficult to detect automatically. A fundamental challenge is the lack of an oracle that specifies the expected rendering of an arbitrary plotting script. Furthermore, an update to one graphic element may inadvertently affect other elements or properties, leading to subtle inconsistencies in the final rendered image.
  This paper presents VIZDETOUR, an automated testing approach for detecting rendering bugs in imperative data visualization libraries via equivalent mutations. The key idea is to transform the oracle problem into an equivalence-checking problem. Starting from a seed plotting script, VIZDETOUR appends a short sequence of semantically equivalent API calls that temporarily modify the visualization state and then restore it to its original state. Although these mutations exercise different execution paths, they should preserve the final rendering. Any visual discrepancy between the original and mutated scripts therefore indicates a rendering bug. To generate such mutations, VIZDETOUR constructs a render tree from the seed script, identifies traceable graphic elements and mutable properties, and synthesizes endpoint-preserving mutation sequences. It then compares the rendered outputs using perceptual hashing. We evaluate VIZDETOUR on matplotlib, bokeh, and plotly using scripts collected from their official example galleries. VIZDETOUR discovers 47 previously unknown bugs, of which 39 are confirmed and 18 are fixed.

</details>


### [7] [Automatic Testing of Interacting Autonomous Vehicles](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12452v2)
*Fabio Cavaleri,Alessio Gambi,Paolo Arcaini,Dejan Ničković,Mauro Pezzè*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出EVITA方法，利用多目标优化生成触发多种AV交互的场景，提高安全关键行为的检测能力。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于场景的测试方法主要测试单个AV，忽略了多AV交互产生的关键行为，且多AV交互导致组合爆炸，需要更有效的测试方法。

Method: 提出EVITA方法，基于多目标优化生成触发多种多样AV交互的场景，同时最小化场景复杂度。

Result: 实验结果表明，EVITA比现有方法引发更多样化的AV交互，提高了揭示安全关键行为的可能性。

Conclusion: EVITA能够有效测试多个交互的AV，揭示被当前方法忽略的安全关键场景。

中文摘要：自动驾驶车辆（AV）必须经过彻底测试以满足高安全标准，避免危及AV乘客和道路使用者。基于场景的测试在虚拟仿真环境中实现驾驶场景，作为现场测试的经济有效的替代方案。常见的基于场景的测试方法设置环境和周围交通，并测试单个AV。最近的研究表明，测试单个AV的方法会遗漏多个AV之间交互产生的关键行为。有效测试由多方交互产生的场景的方法必须解决多AV存在进一步加剧的组合爆炸问题。在本文中，我们提出EVITA，一种利用多目标优化来生成触发多种多样AV交互的场景的方法，同时最小化生成场景的复杂性，以有效测试多个交互的AV并揭示当前方法忽略的安全关键场景。我们在本文中讨论的实验结果证实，EVITA比现有方法引发了更多样化的AV交互，从而提高了揭示安全关键行为的可能性。

Original abstract: Autonomous vehicles (AVs) must be thoroughly tested to meet high safety standards and avoid endangering both AV passengers and road users. Scenario-based testing implements driving scenarios in virtual simulation environments as a cost-effective alternative to field testing. Common scenario-based testing approaches set the environment and the surrounding traffic and test a single AV. Recent studies show that the approaches that test single AVs miss critical behaviors that emerge from interactions among multiple AVs. Effective approaches to test scenarios that emerge from n-way interactions must address the combinatorial explosion that the presence of multiple AVs further exacerbates. In this paper, we propose EVITA, an approach that leverages multi-objective optimization to generate scenarios that trigger multiple and diverse AVs interactions, while minimizing the complexity of the generated scenarios, to effectively test multiple interacting AVs and reveal safety-critical scenarios that current approaches overlook. The experimental results that we discuss in this paper confirm that EVITA triggers a higher variety of AVs interactions than state-of-the-art approaches, thus improving the likelihood to reveal safety-critical behaviors.

### [8] [CodeOwl: Automatic Generation of Tiered Parsons Problems for Introductory Programming](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12460v1)
*Luca Cisternino,Florian Obermüller,Gordon Fraser*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: CodeOwl是一个AI驱动的工具，自动生成分层Parsons问题；评估表明其能有效提升难度，教师和学生认可但希望增加课程控制与反馈机制。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发CodeOwl工具，从样本任务或概念自动生成三层Parsons问题序列；采用混合评估：复杂性分析（297序列）、专家评分清晰度、教师和学生用户研究。

中文摘要：解决编程教育中的学习者异质性具有挑战性，因为学生在速度、先前知识和动机方面存在差异。虽然差异化教学（例如分层序列）允许学生以适当的难度级别参与，但手动创建这些资源是劳动密集型的。本文介绍了CodeOwl，一个AI驱动的工具，可自动生成分层的Parsons问题。从一个样本任务或特定编程概念开始，CodeOwl自动生成分层序列的Parsons问题。我们使用一个混合方法框架评估了CodeOwl，包括复杂性分析、专家评分和用户研究。对297个分层序列（每个三层）的分析显示，98.7%实现了正向的复杂性增加，成功地从第1层到第3层提高了难度。专家评价生成的问题陈述高度清晰。虽然教师称赞该工具的实用性，但他们认为需要对课程对齐有更大的控制权。同样，学生也给出了积极反馈，但要求增强反馈机制和替代交互模式。

Original abstract: Addressing learner heterogeneity in programming education is challenging due to variations in student speed, prior knowledge, and motivation. While differentiated instruction, such as tiered sequences, allows students to engage at appropriate difficulty levels, manually creating these resources is labour-intensive. This paper introduces CodeOwl, an AI-driven tool that automates the generation of tiered Parsons problems. Starting from a sample task or specific programming concepts, CodeOwl produces tiered sequences of Parsons problems automatically. We evaluated CodeOwl with a mixed-method framework comprising complexity analysis, expert ratings, and user studies. Analysis of 297 tiered sequences (three tiers each) revealed that 98.7% achieved a positive complexity increase, successfully rising in difficulty from Tier 1 to Tier 3. Experts rated the generated problem statements as highly clear. While teachers praised the tool's utility, they identified a need for greater control over curriculum alignment. Similarly, students reported positively but requested enhanced feedback mechanisms and alternative interaction modes.

### [9] [Understanding before Naming! Enhancing LLM-based Method Name Prediction with Code Summarization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12467v1)
*Wei Liu,Weisong Sun,Tingting Xu,Hanwei Qian,Yi Zhao,Chunrong Fang,Xia Feng*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过实证研究比较评估器和生成策略，发现基于LLM的评估更符合人类判断，总结-改进策略提升语义质量；提出SMNP方法，结合面向MNP的总结和思维链增强，在多个LLM和数据集上有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法名称预测评估依赖token相似度，不符合人类判断；LLM生成名称直接映射代码到名称，与人类先理解功能再命名的过程不同。

Method: 进行实证研究比较6种度量评估器、5种LLM评估器和6种人类评估器；比较直接生成与总结-改进策略；提出SMNP方法，包含MNP导向的总结和链式思维增强的改进。

Result: LLM评估器（尤其DeepSeek）更符合人类判断；总结-改进策略提升语义质量；SMNP在5个LLM和2个数据集上表现有效且鲁棒。

Conclusion: 基于实证发现提出的SMNP方法能有效提升方法名称预测的语义质量，具有鲁棒性。

中文摘要：方法名称对软件质量至关重要，影响代码的可理解性、可维护性和开发者协作。然而，手动设计有意义的名称具有挑战性。方法名称预测（MNP）从代码片段自动生成方法名称，近期受到关注。尽管大语言模型（LLM）在MNP上表现出色，但仍面临两个挑战：首先，现有评估主要依赖令牌相似性指标，往往无法反映人类对语义质量的判断；其次，当前基于LLM的MNP方法通常通过直接从代码到名称的映射生成名称，这与人类先理解功能再命名的过程不同。为应对这些挑战，我们对基于LLM的评估和MNP策略进行了实证研究。我们比较了6种基于度量的评估器、5种基于LLM的评估器和6种人类评估器。结果表明，基于LLM的评估器（尤其是基于DeepSeek的评估器）比传统指标更符合人类判断。我们进一步比较了直接生成策略与总结-改进策略，结果表明总结与改进通常能提高生成名称的语义质量。案例研究揭示了三个局限：不准确的总结、语义错位和语义分数接近。基于这些发现，我们提出了SMNP，一种结合面向MNP的总结和思维链增强改进的MNP方法。在5个LLM和2个数据集上的实验证明了SMNP的有效性和鲁棒性。

Original abstract: Method names are critical to software quality, affecting code comprehensibility, maintainability, and developer collaboration. However, manually designing meaningful method names is challenging. Method Name Prediction (MNP), which automatically generates method names from code snippets, has recently attracted attention. Although large language models (LLMs) show promising performance for MNP, two challenges remain. First, existing evaluations mainly rely on token similarity metrics, which often fail to reflect human judgments of semantic quality. Second, current LLM-based MNP methods usually generate names through direct code-to-name mapping, which differs from the human process of understanding functionality before naming. To address these challenges, we conduct empirical studies on LLM-based evaluation and MNP strategies. We compare 6 metric-based evaluators, 5 LLM-based evaluators, and 6 human evaluators. Results show that LLM-based evaluators, especially DeepSeek-based evaluators, are more consistent with human judgments than traditional metrics. We further compare direct generation and summarization-and-refinement strategies. Results indicate that summarization and refinement generally improve the semantic quality of generated names. Case studies reveal three limitations: inaccurate summaries, semantic misalignment, and close semantic scores. Based on these findings, we propose SMNP, an MNP approach combining MNP-oriented summarization and chain-of-thought enhanced refinement. Experiments on 5 LLMs and 2 datasets demonstrate the effectiveness and robustness of SMNP.

### [10] [Agent-Safety Evaluations as Load-Bearing Evidence: A Vendor-Neutral, Cross-Harness Reconstructability Metric](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12469v1)
*Oleg Solozobov*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文提出一种属性级可重构性指标和证据充分性卡片，用于评估AI安全决策证据的可重构性，实验表明当前许多轨迹不满足重放前提条件，合成门控测试验证了指标有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前安全评估结果缺乏可靠的证据基础，同类名义结果可能隐藏不同证据质量，但缺少可操作的量化指标来评估证据是否能支撑决策。

Method: 定义八个决策属性类上的可重构性指标，构建跨测试平台适配器输出证据充分性卡片；设计反事实重放协议及重放前提条件探查器，并定义声明-证据过度声明差距。

Result: 在四个表面相同输入上，十二字段充分性范围为0.458-0.833；所有评分的轨迹均未满足重放前提条件；合成门控测试中，原始变体充分性0.542被阻止，仪器化变体0.667通过。

Conclusion: 安全评估声明必须附带可重构性向量，且所有数字应由可复现包重新生成，以确保证据的透明性和可信度。

中文摘要：许多智能体安全评估结果尚未成为可靠的证据：相同的名义结果（任务成功、攻击成功、监控器分数）可能建立在截然不同的证据体系之上。目前尚无供应商中立、可运行的仪器分数重构性评估指标：即捕获的证据能否重构出决策所依赖的决策依据。本文提出了一种基于八个决策属性类的属性级可重构性指标，以及一个跨测试平台的适配器，该适配器为每个决策生成证据充分性卡片，支持每次运行的监控覆盖检查。它指定了一个反事实重放干预协议，实现了其重放前提条件的探查器，并定义了声明-证据过度声明差距。在公开和捆绑的轨迹上，无需新的模型运行，十二字段充分性在四个表面阅读相同的输入上跨度0.458-0.833；重放前提条件在每条评分的轨迹中均未满足。在一个合成发布-门控对中，充分性门控阻止了原始变体（0.542）并通过了仪器化变体（0.667）。安全评估声明应附带其可重构性向量；一个可复现包重新生成每个报告的数字。

Original abstract: Many agent-safety evaluation results are not yet load-bearing evidence: identical nominal outcomes (task success, attack success, monitor scores) may sit atop materially different evidence regimes. No vendor-neutral, runnable instrument scores reconstructability as an evaluation-validity metric: whether captured evidence can reconstruct the decision a claim depends on. This paper introduces a property-level reconstructability metric over eight decision-property classes and a cross-harness adapter emitting per-decision Evidence Sufficiency Cards backing a per-run monitor-coverage release check. It specifies a counterfactual-replay intervention protocol, implements its replayability-precondition probe, and defines a claim-evidence overclaim gap. On public and bundled traces, without new model runs, twelve-field sufficiency spans 0.458-0.833 across four inputs sharing a surface reading; replay preconditions are unmet in every scored trace. In a synthetic release-gate pair, the sufficiency gate blocks the raw variant (0.542) and passes the instrumented (0.667). Safety-evaluation claims should travel with their reconstructability vector; a reproducibility package regenerates every reported number.

### [11] [Taming the Drift: Context-aware Repair of Dockerfile Drift during Software Evolution](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12541v1)
*Chengjie Wang,Jingzheng Wu,Xiang Ling,Tianyue Luo,Chen Zhao*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: Cadre是一个上下文感知的Dockerfile漂移修复框架，利用依赖图引导补丁生成，在1040个实例的基准上实现35.22%修复率，显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Dockerfile漂移修复方法孤立分析Dockerfile，无法处理上下文相关的构建失败，导致CI/CD构建频繁失败。

Method: 提出Cadre框架，通过静态分析构建上下文感知依赖图（CDG），映射指令间和文件级依赖；再基于CDG选择因果相关上下文生成补丁。同时提出DodeX流水线从CI日志中挖掘真实漂移实例。

Result: 在$D^3$基准（1040实例）上修复率35.22%，是规则基线的2.78倍、最佳LLM基线的1.24倍；95.25%提示低于30k token，无提示溢出失败。

Conclusion: 显式依赖建模显著提升上下文感知的IaC维护性能，CDG和两步工作流均有效，且优势随漂移老化而增加。

中文摘要：Docker被广泛用于创建可重现的构建环境，但Dockerfile漂移（Dockerfile与其不断演进的源代码之间的差异）可能导致CI/CD构建失败。现有的基于规则和基于检索的修复方法孤立地分析Dockerfile，因此难以处理上下文相关的失败。我们提出Cadre，一种用于自动修复Dockerfile漂移的上下文感知框架。Cadre使用静态分析构建上下文感知依赖图（CDG），将每个Dockerfile指令映射到其文件级别和指令间依赖关系。在CDG的指导下，Cadre首先选择与失败因果相关的上下文，然后从该上下文生成有针对性的补丁。我们还引入了DodeX，这是一个从GitHub Actions CI日志中挖掘真实世界Dockerfile漂移实例的流水线，同时保留了静态快照数据集所省略的完整构建配置。使用DodeX，我们构建了$D^3$，一个包含1,040个漂移实例的基准测试，这些实例可在本地使用原始CI参数重现。在$D^3$上，Cadre实现了35.22%的修复率，是基于规则基线的2.78倍，以及基于最佳LLM基线的1.24倍。其两步工作流程使95.25%的提示保持在30k token以下，并避免了提示溢出失败——这种失败导致每方法41到58个案例中基于LLM的竞争方法无法生成补丁。消融结果证实，CDG和两步工作流程都提高了修复性能。Cadre相对于仅diff方法的优势也随着漂移跨提交老化而增加，支持了对上下文感知基础设施即代码维护的显式依赖建模。代码和数据可在https://github.com/dw763j/Cadre获取。

Original abstract: Docker is widely used to create reproducible build environments, but Dockerfile drift, the divergence between a Dockerfile and its evolving source code, can cause CI/CD builds to fail. Existing rule-based and retrieval-based repair approaches analyze Dockerfiles in isolation and therefore struggle with context-dependent failures. We present Cadre, a context-aware framework for automated Dockerfile drift repair. Cadre uses static analysis to construct a Context-aware Dependency Graph (CDG), which maps each Dockerfile instruction to its file-level and inter-instruction dependencies. Guided by the CDG, Cadre first selects the context causally relevant to a failure and then generates a targeted patch from that context. We also introduce DodeX, a pipeline that mines real-world Dockerfile drift instances from GitHub Actions CI logs while preserving the complete build configurations omitted by static-snapshot datasets. Using DodeX, we construct $D^3$, a benchmark of 1,040 drift instances reproducible locally with the original CI parameters. Across $D^3$, Cadre achieves a 35.22\% repair rate, 2.78$\times$ that of the rule-based baseline and 1.24$\times$ that of the best LLM-based baseline. Its two-step workflow keeps 95.25\% of prompts below 30k tokens and avoids the prompt-overflow failures that prevent competing LLM-based methods from producing patches in 41 to 58 cases per method. Ablation results confirm that both the CDG and the two-step workflow improve repair performance. Cadre's advantage over diff-only approaches also increases as drift ages across commits, supporting explicit dependency modeling for context-aware infrastructure-as-code maintenance. Code and data are available at https://github.com/dw763j/Cadre.

</details>


### [12] [Evaluation Bias and Epistemic Inequality in Global Software Development](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12563v1)
*Sam Khosravi,Amir H. Payberah*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本研究通过比较东非和西北欧的软件工程师，发现测量绩效与感知能力之间存在差距，欧洲参与者系统性地低估了东非工程师的能力，并观察到不同地区工作方式的互补差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机：探讨全球软件开发中因区域不平等导致的能力评估偏见和公平性问题。

Method: 研究方法：在卢旺达、乌干达、瑞典和荷兰开展现场混合方法研究，结合编程、系统设计和代码审查任务与半结构化访谈，涉及48名软件工程师。

Result: 研究结果：东非高级工程师的绩效与欧洲同行相当，但欧洲参与者系统性地低估了东非工程师的能力；不同地区在沟通和组织实践上存在互补差异。

Conclusion: 研究结论：全球软件开发中存在公平性挑战，能力评估受到区域偏见的影响，需要更公正的评估机制。

中文摘要：本文探讨了全球软件开发中的公平与问责问题，聚焦于在不平等的区域背景下如何评估和重视能力。我们比较了来自东非（卢旺达和乌干达）和西北欧（瑞典和荷兰）的软件工程师，这些地区之间的联系日益紧密，但嵌入在不对称的技术、经济和制度结构中。尽管非洲技术生态系统快速增长，但在这些背景下关于日常工程实践和评估的实证证据仍然有限。我们展示了一项在四个国家对48名软件工程师进行的现场混合方法研究的结果。该研究结合了编程、系统设计和代码审查任务以及半结构化访谈。我们的结果揭示了测量绩效与感知能力之间的一致差距。卢旺达的高级工程师通常表现出与欧洲同行相当的水平，但欧洲参与者系统地低估了东非工程师的能力。我们还观察到不同地区在沟通风格和组织实践上的差异，反映了不同但互补的工作方式。

Original abstract: This paper examines fairness and accountability in global software development by focusing on how competence is assessed and valued across unequal regional contexts. We compare software engineers from East Africa (Rwanda and Uganda) and Northwestern Europe (Sweden and the Netherlands), regions that are increasingly connected but embedded in asymmetric technological, economic, and institutional structures. Despite the rapid growth of African technology ecosystems, empirical evidence on everyday engineering practice and evaluation in these contexts remains limited. We present findings from an on-site mixed-methods study with 48 software engineers across four countries. The study combines programming, system design, and code review tasks with semi-structured interviews. Our results reveal consistent gaps between measured performance and perceived competence. Senior engineers in Rwanda often performed at a level comparable to that of their European peers, yet European participants systematically underestimated the competence of East African engineers. We also observed differences in communication styles and organizational practices across regions, reflecting distinct but complementary ways of working.

### [13] [Hierarchical Fault Localization for Autonomous Driving Systems with Hypothesis Validation and Intent Analysis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12598v1)
*Rui Zheng,Changwen Li,Yi Ji,Rongjie Yan*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: HINT是一个两阶段分层故障定位框架，通过因果推理和可靠性感知的一致性检查，在自动驾驶系统中实现从模块级到代码级的根因定位，端到端Class@5准确率达77.8%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ADS故障定位技术只能检测系统级故障或归因到粗粒度模块，无法定位源代码根因，导致调试劳动密集。

Method: 两阶段框架：Phase I将故障触发记录转为多模态抽象，用因果推理识别责任模块；Phase II重建设计意图和实现行为，通过可靠性感知一致性检查定位可疑代码。

Result: 在Apollo上模块级诊断和代码级定位指标最强，端到端Class@5准确率77.8%。

Conclusion: HINT有效提升了ADS故障定位的精度和效率，无需重模拟即可定位代码级根因。

中文摘要：全面测试对于自动驾驶系统（ADS）的安全性和可靠性至关重要。现有技术可以检测系统级故障或将故障归因于粗粒度模块，但通常无法定位源代码中的根本原因。因此，调试仍然需要大量人工，要求开发者将行为违规与复杂的实现逻辑联系起来。为解决这一差距，我们提出了HINT，一个基于假设验证和意图分析的两阶段分层ADS故障定位框架。在第一阶段，HINT将触发故障的执行记录转换为多模态抽象，并使用因果推理识别责任模块。在第二阶段，它重建设计方意图和实现方行为，然后通过可靠性感知的一致性检查定位可疑代码，无需昂贵的重模拟。我们在Apollo上针对不同故障模式和模块评估了HINT。结果表明，HINT在模块级诊断和代码级定位指标上达到了最强的整体性能，在真实世界漏洞上的端到端Class@5准确率为77.8%。

Original abstract: Comprehensive testing is essential for the safety and reliability of Autonomous Driving Systems (ADS). Existing techniques can detect system-level failures or attribute them to coarse-grained modules, but they often fall short of localizing the root cause in source code. As a result, debugging remains labor-intensive, requiring developers to connect behavioral violations with complex implementation logic. To address this gap, we present HINT, a two-phase framework for hierarchical ADS fault localization based on hypothesis validation and intent analysis. In Phase I, HINT transforms failure-triggering execution recordings into multi-modal abstractions and uses causal reasoning to identify the responsible module. In Phase II, it reconstructs design-side intent and implementation-side behavior, then localizes suspicious code through reliability-aware consistency checking, without costly re-simulation. We evaluate HINT on Apollo across diverse failure modes and modules. The results show that HINT achieves the strongest overall performance across module-level diagnosis and code-level localization metrics, with 77.8% end-to-end Class@5 accuracy on real-world bugs.

### [14] [Multi-Perspective Agentic Program Repair via Code Property Graphs and Temporal Execution Graphs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12605v1)
*Zhili Huang,Ling Xu,Hongyu Zhang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出CT-Repair框架，通过结构化运行时证据和多视角推理提升程序自动修复效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM-based APR存在执行轨迹过大重复和补丁采样缺乏多样性两个局限。

Method: 构建CPG和TEG，通过三阶段过滤压缩TEG，三个有限状态机智能体从静态、动态、混合角度分析并生成修复策略，策略引导补丁生成与优化。

Result: 在854个Defects4J错误上，混合模型修复489个，GPT-5.4-mini配置下修复388个，优于基线；多视角联合比单视角多修复99个；过滤大幅压缩证据。

Conclusion: 结构化运行时证据和多视角推理能提升修复效果，无需依赖更大补丁生成预算。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）改进了自动化程序修复（APR），但仍存在两个限制。首先，原始执行轨迹通常过大且重复，无法作为有效的模型上下文。其次，重复的补丁采样可能产生不同的实现，但不会产生不同的根因假设或修复策略。我们提出了CT-Repair，一种基于智能体的APR框架，将静态和动态证据表示为可查询的代码属性图（CPG）和时间执行图（TEG）。CT-Repair应用一个三阶段过滤流水线来构建紧凑的TEG。三个有限状态机引导的智能体分别从静态、动态和混合角度分析每个错误，并独立生成基于证据的修复策略。策略引导的生成过程将这些策略实例化为候选补丁，并使用验证反馈来优化最有潜力的策略。我们在Defects4J v3.0的854个Java错误上评估了CT-Repair。在混合模型配置下，CT-Repair正确修复了489个错误。在受控的GPT-5.4-mini配置下，它修复了388个错误，分别比ReinFix和RepairAgent多19个和30个。三种证据视角的联合比最强的单一视角多修复了99个错误。过滤流水线还压缩了运行时证据，执行过滤平均将候选方法范围缩小了94.85%，行为过滤进一步将保留的运行时记录减少了55.97%。这些结果表明，结构化的运行时证据和多视角推理可以在不单纯依赖更大的补丁生成预算的情况下提高修复效果。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have improved automated program repair (APR), but two limitations remain. First, raw execution traces are often too large and repetitive to serve as effective model context. Second, repeated patch sampling may produce different implementations without yielding distinct root-cause hypotheses or repair strategies. We present CT-Repair, an agentic APR framework representing static and dynamic evidence as queryable Code Property Graph (CPG) and Temporal Execution Graph (TEG). CT-Repair applies a three-stage filtering pipeline to construct compact TEGs. Three finite-state-machine-guided agents analyze each bug from static, dynamic, and hybrid perspectives and independently produce evidence-grounded repair strategies. A strategy-guided generation procedure instantiates these strategies as candidate patches and uses validation feedback to refine the most promising strategy.
  We evaluate CT-Repair on 854 Java bugs from Defects4J v3.0. In the mixed-model configuration, CT-Repair correctly repairs 489 bugs. Under a controlled GPT-5.4-mini configuration, it repairs 388 bugs, 19 and 30 more than ReinFix and RepairAgent, respectively. The union of the three evidence perspectives repairs 99 more bugs than the strongest individual perspective. The filtering pipeline also compacts runtime evidence, with execution filtering narrowing the candidate method scope by 94.85% on average and behavior filtering further reducing retained runtime records by 55.97%. These results show that structured runtime evidence and multi-perspective reasoning can improve repair effectiveness without relying solely on a larger patch-generation budget.

### [15] [SemaDiff: Identifying Semantic-Changing Commits with Generated Code and Tests](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13111v1)
*Maha Ayub,Michael Konstantinou,Ahmed Khanfir,Nikolaos Tsantalis,Mike Papadakis*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出SemaDiff方法，通过比较提交前后版本的测试执行行为来识别语义保留提交，利用大语言模型生成额外依赖代码并进行自动测试，在183个Java项目提交数据集上达到76%准确率和100%语义更改提交检测精确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有重构检测方法无法确保提交纯语义保留，影响调试、故障定位等任务，需要能区分语义保留与更改提交的方法。

Method: SemaDiff分析代码差异，提取未变更的依赖代码，用大语言模型生成额外的依赖类，自动生成测试，比较两个版本上测试结果是否一致以分类提交。

Result: 在183个提交数据集上，语义保留/更改区分准确率约76%，语义更改提交检测精确率100%。

Conclusion: SemaDiff能有效区分语义保留与语义更改提交，且语义更改检测无假阳性，有助于软件仓库挖掘任务。

中文摘要：区分语义保留提交和语义更改提交仍然是软件仓库挖掘中的一个开放挑战。现有方法能够准确检测重构提交，但无法确保提交是纯粹的语义保留，没有任何交织的行为更改修改。这一限制可能影响多个任务，如调试、故障定位、错误数据集构建、回滚分析和错误修复的回溯移植。为填补这一空白，我们提出SemaDiff，一种通过基于行为的分析来识别语义保留提交的新方法；比较提交前后版本中类似测试的执行。由于受重构影响的代码通常难以测试，并且在两个版本中不同，我们提出为这些代码生成额外的调用方法，作为测试目标。给定一个提交，SemaDiff分析差异以识别修改的代码，并提取调用它的未变更的依赖代码。然后，它使用大型语言模型生成一个额外的依赖类，以在两个版本中执行更改后的代码，并自动为依赖代码生成测试。这样，我们为不同代码版本获得相同的测试，从而实现行为差异检测。只有当所有生成的测试在两个版本中产生相同结果时，该提交才被分类为语义保留。为了评估SemaDiff，我们构建并手动标注了一个包含183个提交的数据集，这些提交来自知名的开源Java项目。获得的结果表明，SemaDiff能够准确区分语义保留和语义更改的提交，准确率约为76%，在语义更改提交检测上达到了100%的精确率。

Original abstract: Distinguishing semantic-preserving commits from changing ones remains an open challenge in software repository mining. While existing approaches detect refactoring commits accurately, they cannot ensure that a commit is purely semantic-preserving, without any interleaving behaviour-changing modification. This limitation can impact several tasks, such as debugging, fault localisation, bug dataset construction, rollback analysis, and bug fixes backporting. To fill this gap, we propose SemaDiff, a novel approach for identifying semantic-preserving commits through behaviour-based analysis; comparison of similar test execution on pre- and post-commit versions. As code impacted by the refactoring is often hard to test and different accross both versions, we propose generating additional calling methods to that code, which serve as testing target. Given a commit, SemaDiff analyses the diff to identify modified code and extracts unchanged dependent code that calls it. It then generates an additional dependent class using a large language model to exercise the changed code in both versions, and automatically generates tests for the dependent code. This way, we obtain the same tests for the different code versions, enabling the behavioural-difference detection. The commit is classified as semantic-preserving only if all generated tests produce identical outcomes across the two versions. To evaluate SemaDiff, we construct and annotate manually a dataset of 183 commits, gathered from well-known open-source Java projects. The obtained results show that SemaDiff distinguishes accurately semantic-preserving from -- changing commits in about 76% of the cases, with a 100% precision in semantic-changing commit detection.

</details>


### [16] [Line-Anchored Feedback Cuts Token Costs and Improves Correctness in AI Code Editing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12713v1)
*William Franz Lamberti*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 基于行的锚定反馈能显著减少GAI代码编辑中的令牌生成（最高58%），并提升正确性（特别是弱模型和大文件）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成的令牌直接影响GAI代码编辑的成本、延迟和能耗，而反馈格式是一个未被充分探索的优化杠杆。

Method: 通过VSCodium扩展FileMark实现行锚定反馈，与整体提示进行配对实验，并探索由工具而非模型应用补丁的效果。

Result: 令牌生成减少22%-80%，正确性提升2-7分；在100行以上文件中，本地模型正确性在锚定下翻三倍。

Conclusion: 行锚定反馈是一种有效的优化手段，既能降低强模型的资源消耗，又能提升弱模型的性能。

中文摘要：生成的令牌是生成式人工智能（GAI）代码编辑中成本、延迟和能耗的直接驱动力。我们展示了反馈格式是对这三者的杠杆。我们比较了相同请求变更的两种交付方式：整体提示（对照）与结构化、基于行的FileMark导出（处理）。FileMark是一个用于对任意文件进行内联注释的VSCodium扩展。在一项配对实验中，基于行的锚定将生成的令牌减少了22%（Claude Opus）和58%（Claude Sonnet），在100行或以上的文件中达到24%-80%，经过多重检验校正后，七个模型中有四个生成的令牌显著减少。在模型有提升空间的情况下，正确性有所提高：整体+2.0分，三个本地模型中的五个提高5-7分。一项探索性实验中，由工具而非GAI模型应用函数级补丁，显示当编辑应用负担被移除时，正确性进一步提升：在100行以上文件中，本地模型的正确性在锚定下大约翻了三倍。基于行的锚定减少了强模型的消耗，提高了弱模型的正确性。

Original abstract: Generated tokens are a direct driver of the cost, latency, and energy of generative AI (GAI) code editing. We show the format of feedback is a lever on all three. We compare two deliveries of the same requested changes: a holistic prompt (control) versus the structured, line-anchored export of FileMark (treatment). FileMark is a VSCodium extension for inline comments on any file. In a paired experiment line anchoring cut generated tokens by 22% (Claude Opus) and 58% (Claude Sonnet), reaching 24%-80% on files of 100 lines or more, with four of seven models generating significantly fewer tokens after multiple-testing correction. Correctness rose where models had headroom: +2.0 points pooled and +5 to +7 points for three of five local models. An exploratory experiment in which the harness, not the GAI model, applies function-level patches shows the correctness benefit grows further when the edit-application burden is lifted: local-model correctness on 100+ line files roughly triples under anchoring. Line-anchored feedback reduces what stronger models spend and improves what weaker models get right.

### [17] [Toward Localizing and Repairing Bias in Transformer Attention Heads](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12863v1)
*Sigma Jahan*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出ROBIN，一种白盒头级公平性调试方法，通过推理时干预定位和修复注意力头中的偏见，实验表明能有效降低WinoBias差距并保持语言建模质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法难以在模型内部定位和修复偏见，且偏置行为可能集中在少量注意力头上，因此需要更精细的推理时干预方法。

Method: ROBIN方法：利用公平性探针的敏感性对注意力头排序，并移除选定头输出中的小偏见子空间。

Result: 在四个模型的实验中，ROBIN在所有模型上降低了WinoBias差距，且语言建模质量优于整个头归零方法。

Conclusion: 头级偏见修复需同时考虑头的选择和修改方式，ROBIN提供了一种有效的推理时修复框架。

中文摘要：Transformer语言模型越来越多地用作软件组件，但有偏输出仍然难以在模型内部定位和修复。现有的公平性测试和修复方法主要在输入-输出或重新训练级别操作，而最近的研究表明，与偏见相关的行为可以集中在少量注意力头上。本文研究是否可以通过针对性的推理时干预来定位和修复注意力头。我们提出了ROBIN，一种白盒头级公平性调试方法，该方法使用对公平性探针的敏感性对注意力头进行排序，并从选定的头输出中移除一个小的偏见子空间。在一项四模型试点研究中，ROBIN在所有模型上减少了测量的WinoBias差距，同时比整个头归零更好地保持了语言建模质量。这些初步结果表明，头级偏见修复不仅应考虑选择哪些头，还应考虑如何修改选定的头。

Original abstract: Transformer language models are increasingly used as software components, yet biased outputs remain difficult to localize and repair inside the model. Existing fairness testing and repair methods largely operate at the input-output or retraining level, while recent work suggests that bias-related behavior can concentrate in a small set of attention heads. This paper studies whether attention heads can be localized and repaired through a targeted inference-time intervention. We introduce ROBIN, a white-box head-level fairness debugging method that ranks attention heads using sensitivity to fairness probes and removes a small bias subspace from selected head outputs. In a four-model pilot study, ROBIN reduces the measured WinoBias gap across all models while preserving language-modeling quality better than whole-head zeroing. These preliminary results suggest that head-level bias repair should consider not only which heads are selected, but also how selected heads are modified.

### [18] [Deep4ge: DNN Training Trajectories for Fault Detection and Diagnosis](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12868v1)
*Sigma Jahan*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: Deep4ge是一个包含14,227次训练运行（9,845次故障，4,382次基线）的受控基准数据集，支持深度学习系统的故障检测、诊断和早期预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软件工程社区缺乏公开的逐周期训练运行数据集，这些数据集应带有记录故障历史、特征提取细节和清晰复用支持，用于故障检测和诊断任务。

Method: 从Stack Overflow收集59个改编的TensorFlow/Keras DNN程序，使用27种源代码转换引入七类已知故障，生成14,227次训练运行，并记录每次运行的4个评估指标和26个逐周期特征（权重、梯度、激活值、准确率和损失趋势、学习率、硬件使用）。

Result: 创建了包含9,845次故障运行和4,382次正确基线运行的数据集，支持二元故障检测、多类故障诊断和基于部分训练运行的早期预测。

Conclusion: Deep4ge提供了数据集和故障注入框架，可促进深度学习系统故障检测和诊断的研究与评估。

中文摘要：深度学习系统常常因为改变训练行为的细微实现故障而失败。最近的工作研究了如何从训练周期中观察到的变化来检测和诊断此类故障。然而，软件工程社区仍然缺乏一个公开的、包含逐周期训练运行数据、带有记录故障历史、特征提取细节和清晰复用支持的数据集，用于故障检测和诊断任务。我们提出了Deep4ge，一个受控的基准测试，包含从Stack Overflow收集的59个改编的TensorFlow/Keras深度神经网络（DNN）程序生成的14,227次训练运行。我们使用了27种源代码转换来引入已知的故障，涵盖七类。该数据集包含9,845次故障运行和4,382次正确基线运行。对于每次运行，我们记录了4个评估指标和26个测量每个周期训练行为的特征。这些特征捕获了权重、梯度、激活值、准确率和损失趋势、学习率以及硬件使用情况。Deep4ge支持二元故障检测、多类故障诊断以及从部分训练运行中提前预测故障。我们在https://doi.org/10.5281/zenodo.20337241上发布了数据集和故障注入框架。

Original abstract: Deep learning systems often fail due to subtle implementation faults that alter training behavior. Recent work has studied how to detect and diagnose such failures from changes observed across training epochs. However, the software engineering community still lacks a public dataset of per-epoch training runs with documented fault history, feature extraction details, and clear reuse support for fault detection and diagnosis tasks. We present Deep4ge, a controlled benchmark of 14,227 training runs generated from 59 adapted TensorFlow/Keras deep neural network (DNN) programs collected from Stack Overflow. We generated faulty variants using 27 source-code transformations that introduce known faults across seven categories. The dataset contains 9,845 faulty runs and 4,382 correct baseline runs. For each run, we record 4 evaluation metrics and 26 features that measure training behavior at every epoch. These features capture weights, gradients, activations, accuracy and loss trends, learning rate, and hardware use. Deep4ge supports binary fault detection, multi-class fault diagnosis, and early fault prediction from partial training runs. We release the dataset and fault-injection framework at https://doi.org/10.5281/zenodo.20337241.

</details>


### [19] [Salesforce Messaging Architecture: Platform Events, Async Sends, and Multi-Tenancy at Scale](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12943v1)
*Devam Gupta*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出在CRM内部原生构建消息核心的架构，以解决传统外部连接器导致的隔离问题，并基于生产托管包评估其可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统企业消息集成作为外部连接器，导致消息与CRM记录隔离，依赖脆弱的同步和映射，存在一致性问题。

Method: 构建在CRM内部原生运行的消息核心，使消息成为原生CRM记录，出站路径作为原生事务，状态参数存储为标准数据库对象，并利用平台原生管道和自动化。

Result: 通过在生产环境中跨多个行业的托管包部署，评估了核心设计模式、扩展机制、多租户约束和平台原生架构的边界。

Conclusion: 该原生架构能有效对齐CRM平台，消除隔离，提升集成可靠性和自动化能力，但需考虑平台限制和多租户约束。

中文摘要：大多数企业消息集成功能作为外部连接器运行。它们驻留在客户关系管理（CRM）平台之外，接收webhook，编写外围日志，并认为过程已集成。因此，消息在消息平台内孤立，而CRM记录严格保留在CRM内部，仅通过脆弱的同步作业、僵化的字段映射和最终一致性窗口连接。本文概述了一种替代架构范式：在CRM内部原生构建整个消息核心。在这种模型中，每条消息被视为原生CRM记录，每个出站路径是平台原生事务，所有状态参数——包括传递状态、选择加入指标、对话历史和记录所有权——都作为标准数据库对象存储。这种结构上的原生对齐允许系统利用标准报告管道，在原生工作流构建器内操作，并无缝触发平台自动化。基于部署在跨独立企业组织（涵盖医疗保健、销售运营、现场服务和客户支持）的生产托管包，本研究评估了核心设计模式、平台扩展机制、多租户解耦约束以及平台原生架构设计的边界。

Original abstract: Most enterprise messaging integrations function as external connectors. They reside outside the Customer Relationship Management (CRM) platform, receive webhooks, write peripheral logs, and consider the process integrated. Consequently, messages are isolated within the messaging platform while CRM records remain strictly inside the CRM, bridged only by fragile sync jobs, rigid field mappings, and eventual consistency windows. This paper outlines an alternative architectural paradigm: constructing the entire messaging core natively inside the CRM. Within this model, every message is treated as a native CRM record,every outbound path is a platform-native transaction, and all state parameters - including delivery status, opt-in metrics, conversation history, and record ownership - are stored as standard database objects. This structural native alignment allows the system to utilize standard reporting pipelines, operate inside native workflow builders, and trigger platform automation seamlessly. Drawing from a production managed package deployed across independent enterprise organizations spanning healthcare, sales operations, field services, and customer support, this study evaluates the core design patterns, platform scaling mechanics, multi-tenant decoupling constraints, and the boundaries of the platform-native architectural design.

</details>


### [20] [Form, Not Content? A Preregistered, Placebo-Controlled Evaluation of Learned Error-Conditioned Self-Repair Through Prompts and Weights in Frozen Small Code Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12962v1)
*Mehmet Iscan*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出PoPE方法，发现小代码模型无法利用错误信息进行自我修复，证据表明模型操作化使用证伪证据的能力与安慰剂无显著差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自我修复文献缺乏安慰剂对照，无法确定模型是否真正从错误信息中学习。

Method: 引入PoPE（波普尔安慰剂对照评估），通过提示通道和权重通道对冻结的小代码模型进行安慰剂对照实验，使用内容消融和SHA扰乱安慰剂。

Result: 提示通道中内容消融安慰剂解锁12单元 vs 错误模式10单元（机制无效）；权重通道中错误适配器与基线8-8平局，SHA安慰剂10单元领先，未证实内容可归因优势。

Conclusion: 模型将来自神谕的表示写回生成状态，测试被条件作用取代，不能将对抗信息作为外部批评使用；PoPE作为测量标准。

中文摘要：冻结的小代码LLMs本地部署，但在自我修复文献中，失败尝试后重试的指导信息仍然在没有安慰剂对照的情况下进行测量。我们将失败程序视为猜想，执行反例作为相对于神谕的反驳，并引入PoPE（波普尔安慰剂对照评估）：一种用于衡量证伪LLM生成代码的证据是否可以被同一模型操作化使用的方法。在PoPE中，错误内容与通道特定的安慰剂配对，保持预先声明的脚手架，同时消融任务相关内容或扰乱任务-错误分配。冻结的小代码模型（0.5-1.5B）在预先注册的规则下通过提示通道和权重通道（小数据适配器训练）进行评估，每个臂-单元对生成四次。在提示通道中，公开层级筛选在内容消融形式的安慰剂下解锁了12个单元，而在活动错误模式臂下解锁了10个单元，针对40个单元的抵抗带；结果记录为机制无效。在权重通道中，错误内容适配器与无干预基线之间观察到8-8平局（p=1.0），而SHA扰乱的安慰剂适配器保持领先，解锁10个单元；内容可归因的优势未得到确认。这些结果不构成等效性或非劣效性的证据。等效性未单独测试。发现仅限于公开层级筛选终点；隐藏层级确认因设计而推迟。我们将其解读为并非编译的批评作为信息消失，而是其在新猜想测试中的外部作用丧失：当从神谕学到的表示被写回生成状态时，测试被条件作用取代。没有声称工作JEPA-RL控制器。PoPE被提出作为一种安慰剂对照、可重测的测量标准。

Original abstract: Frozen small code LLMs are deployed locally, yet the information guiding a retry after a failed attempt is still measured without placebo controls in the self-repair literature. We treat a failed program as a conjecture and an execution counterexample as an oracle-relative refutation, and introduce PoPE (Popperian Placebo-controlled Evaluation): a methodology for measuring whether evidence that falsifies LLM-generated code can be used operationally by that same model. In PoPE, error content is paired with channel-specific placebos that keep the predeclared scaffold while ablating task-relevant content or deranging the task-error assignment. Frozen small code models (0.5-1.5B) are evaluated under preregistered rules through a prompt channel and a weight channel (small-data adapter training), with four generations per arm-unit pair. In the prompt channel, public-tier screening unlocked 12 units under the content-ablated form placebo versus 10 under the live error-pattern arm on a 40-unit resistant band; the result was recorded as mechanism-null. In the weight channel, an 8-8 tie was observed between the error-content adapter and the intervention-free baseline (p=1.0), while the SHA-deranged placebo adapter stayed ahead with 10 unlocks; content-attributable superiority was not confirmed. These results do not constitute evidence of equivalence or non-inferiority. Equivalence was not tested separately. Findings are restricted to the public-tier screening endpoint; hidden-tier confirmation was deferred by design. We read this not as compiled criticism disappearing as information, but as the loss of its external role in testing a new conjecture: when a representation learned from the oracle is written back into the generation state, testing is replaced by conditioning. No working JEPA-RL controller is claimed. PoPE is presented as a placebo-controlled, retestable measurement standard.

</details>


### [21] [Software Supply Chains are Dead: Use-Case-Oriented Regeneration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13021v1)
*Tanmay Singla,James C. Davis*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出以用例为导向的再生范式，通过合成特定依赖功能切片降低供应链风险并减少API表面，实验表明可行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统依赖模式成本因供应链攻击上升，而生成式AI降低了本地实现成本，促使新范式。

Method: 评估一种代理工作流，仅合成仓库所依赖的特定功能切片。

Result: 在180个仓库-依赖对中，替换保留了99.8%的观测行为，减少了93%的导出API表面。

Conclusion: 软件采购可向可验证的仓库特定代码合成发展，适用于狭窄、稳定且测试良好的功能。

中文摘要：现代软件工程的前提日益令人怀疑：前期通过采用依赖关系节省的实施成本是否大于其维护成本。两个变化正在重塑构建与复用的权衡：软件供应链攻击提高了外部依赖的成本，而生成式人工智能降低了本地实施的成本。我们设想了一种以用例为导向的再生（use-case-oriented regeneration）作为新的软件采购范式，将供应链从外部信任转移到本地验证。我们评估了一个代理工作流，它只合成仓库所依赖的特定功能切片。我们对180个仓库-依赖对进行的测量表明，这种方法可行：替换后，保留了仓库在基线验证检查中观察到的行为的99.8%，并减少了93%的导出API表面。软件采购可能朝着可验证的仓库特定代码合成方向发展，尤其是在所需功能狭窄、稳定且经过良好测试的情况下。

Original abstract: Modern software development relies on an increasingly doubtful premise: that the up-front implementation savings from adopting a dependency outweighs the maintenance costs. Two changes are reshaping the build-vs.-reuse calculus: software supply chain attacks have raised the cost of external reliance, while generative AI has lowered the cost of local implementation. We envision use-case-oriented regeneration as a new software sourcing paradigm that shifts the supply chain from external trust to local verification. We evaluate an agentic workflow that synthesizes only the specific slice of dependency functionality that a repository exercises. Our measurements across 180 repository-dependency pairs suggest that this approach is feasible: the replacements preserve 99.8% of repository-observed behavior across baseline validation checks and reduce the exported API surface by 93%. Software sourcing may evolve toward verifiable repository-specific code synthesis, especially when the required functionality is narrow, stable, and well tested.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在巴西一家大型企业进行对照实验，比较手动开发、仅DS开发和DS感知AI辅助开发在Angular、iOS和Android技术栈上的效果，进行两个实验周期。

中文摘要：设计系统（DS）有助于标准化前端开发，但开发人员将高保真原型转换为一致、可投入生产的界面时仍面临挑战。尽管AI辅助工具已成为潜在的解决方案，但关于其在以DS为中心的工作流程中有效性的实证证据仍然有限。本文报告了在巴西一家大型企业进行的对照实验，该实验比较了在Angular、iOS和Android技术栈上的手动开发、仅DS开发和DS感知AI辅助开发。两个实验周期的结果表明，AI辅助显著缩短了交付时间（46.7%至69.4%），提高了任务完成度，并减少了性能变异性。对中断模式的分析进一步表明，工作流摩擦减少，任务执行更顺畅。这些发现提供了实证证据，表明DS感知AI工具可以显著加速开发，提高设计保真度，并为工业前端工作流程带来实际效益。

Original abstract: Design Systems (DS) help standardize front-end development, yet developers still face challenges when translating high-fidelity mockups into consistent, production-ready interfaces. Although AI-assisted tools have emerged as a potential solution, empirical evidence on their effectiveness within DS-centered workflows remains limited. This paper reports a controlled experiment conducted at a large Brazilian enterprise that compares manual development, DS-only development, and DS-aware AI-assisted development across Angular, iOS, and Android stacks. Results from two experimental cycles show that AI assistance significantly reduced time-to-delivery (by 46.7% to 69.4%), increased task completeness, and decreased performance variability. Analysis of break patterns further suggests reduced workflow friction and smoother task execution. These findings provide empirical evidence that DS-aware AI tools can significantly accelerate development, improve design fidelity, and yield practical benefits for industrial front-end workflows.

### [23] [From Human-Centric to Agentic Code Review: The Impact of Different Generations of Generative AI Technology on Review Quality](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13196v1)
*Suzhen Zhong,Shayan Noei,Bram Adams,Ying Zou*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 研究AI代码审查时代下，不同AI采用模式对审查效率和质量的实证影响，发现代理协作模式提高效率但不提高质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管AI审查者开始参与代码审查，但缺乏关于这种转变如何影响审查效率和质量的实证证据。

Method: 分析207个GitHub项目的102万次拉取请求，识别三种AI采用实践（渐进式AI采用、快速LLM采用、快速AI代理采用），并将审查讨论建模为审查者交互序列。

Result: 代理协作模式（特别是AI代理发起或多代理审查）在渐进式AI采用和快速AI代理采用下与更快的审查决策相关，但效率提升未转化为更好的审查质量；人机协作模式成为审查效率的最强解释因素。

Conclusion: 为设计高效且不降低质量的AI支持代码审查流程提供实证指导。

中文摘要：代码审查有助于在代码集成之前保持软件质量，但也给人工审查者带来了沉重的工作量。随着生成式人工智能成为软件开发的一部分，代码审查正在从主要是人工审查的过程转向人工智能支持的审查过程，其中大型语言模型（LLM）审查者和AI代理审查者与人工审查者一起参与。然而，我们仍然缺乏关于这种转变如何影响审查效率和审查质量的实证证据。在本文中，我们研究了来自207个GitHub项目的102万次审查过的拉取请求，这些项目跨越了三个代码审查时代：以人为中心的审查、LLM辅助审查和代理式代码审查。我们识别出三种AI审查者采用实践：渐进式AI采用、快速LLM采用和快速AI代理采用。我们进一步将拉取请求审查讨论建模为审查者交互序列，以描述人工、LLM和AI代理审查者在审查过程中如何协作。我们的结果表明，涉及代理的协作模式，特别是由AI代理发起或涉及多个AI代理的审查，与在渐进式AI采用和快速AI代理采用下更快的审查决策相关。然而，这些效率提升并未转化为更好的审查质量。我们还发现，审查活动和拉取请求类型在各个时代仍然重要，而一旦LLM和AI代理审查者参与，人机协作模式成为审查效率的最强解释因素。这些发现为设计能够提高效率而不削弱审查质量的人工智能支持的代码审查流程提供了实证指导。

Original abstract: Code review helps maintain software quality before code integration, but it also imposes a substantial workload on human reviewers. As generative artificial intelligence becomes part of software development, code review is shifting from a primarily human review process toward AI-supported review processes in which large language model (LLM) reviewers and AI agent reviewers participate alongside human reviewers. However, we still lack empirical evidence on how this transition affects review efficiency and review quality. In this paper, we study 1.02 million reviewed pull requests from 207 GitHub projects that transition across three code review eras: human-centric review, LLM-assisted review, and agentic code review. We identify three AI reviewer adoption practices: Gradual AI Adoption, Rapid LLM Adoption, and Rapid AI Agent Adoption. We further model pull request review discussions as reviewer interaction sequences to characterize how human, LLM, and AI agent reviewers collaborate during the review process. Our results show that agent-involved collaboration patterns, especially reviews initiated by AI agents or involving multiple AI agents, are associated with faster review decisions under Gradual AI Adoption and Rapid AI Agent Adoption. However, these efficiency gains do not translate into better review quality. We also find that review activity and pull request type remain important across eras, while human-AI collaboration patterns become the strongest explanatory factor for review efficiency once LLM and AI agent reviewers participate. These findings provide empirical guidance for designing AI-supported code review processes that improve efficiency without weakening review quality.

### [24] [Beyond Object Validation: Relational Conformance in Multi-Artifact Agent Releases](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14155v1)
*Tengjiao Liu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 论文研究了系统验证中最终软件包逃脱审查的故障类，提出了Schema-SIP关系符合性配置文件（SIP-RC），将发布建模为图以确保可追溯性，并展示了其实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有验证机制对输入、工具调用和生成对象进行了检查，但最终软件包往往没有被同等审查，导致自相矛盾的发布，需要建立故障类并设计更严格的验证方法。

Method: 通过分析DRSS发布、Schema Docs和Brand Shuttle GEO中的具体失败案例，提出SIP-RC配置文件，将发布建模为图，包含声明到证据的链接、有限权限决策、派生制品的执行条件和谱系，以及发布字节与检查包的一致性。

Result: 建立了故障类别，并验证了若干机制（如分离验证路径、不可平均化硬故障）的实用性，但完整配置文件的性能优势尚未实验验证。

Conclusion: SIP-RC提供了解决最终包审查缺失问题的候选方案，但其整体有效性需进一步实验检验。

中文摘要：代理系统验证输入、工具调用和生成的对象。最终的软件包往往逃脱了同样的审查。在一次DRSS发布中，账本支持了60分和一个失败的证书；报告宣布了一个100分的Gold Path。每个本地门都是绿灯。该软件包自相矛盾。我们研究了那个失败以及Schema Docs（其中类似的故障变成了产品合同）和Brand Shuttle GEO（其中证据被转化为修复工作）。结果是一个候选的Schema-SIP关系符合性配置文件（SIP-RC）。它将发布建模为一个图：声明指向证据，决策带有有限权限，派生制品保留其执行条件和谱系，发布的字节必须与经过检查的软件包匹配。硬故障不能被平均化，验证器在单独路径上重新计算关键决策。论文建立了故障类别，并展示了若干机制是实用的。完整配置文件是否比现有检查表现更好仍是一个开放的实验。

Original abstract: Agent systems validate inputs, tool calls, and generated objects. The final package often escapes the same scrutiny. In one DRSS release, the ledger supported 60 points and a failed certificate; the report announced a 100-point Gold Path. Every local gate was green. The package contradicted itself.
  We study that failure alongside Schema Docs, where similar faults became product contracts, and Brand Shuttle GEO, where evidence is turned into repair work. The result is a candidate Schema-SIP Relational Conformance profile (SIP-RC). It models a release as a graph: claims point to evidence, decisions carry bounded authority, derived artifacts retain their execution conditions and lineage, and published bytes must match the package that was checked. Hard failures cannot be averaged away, and a validator recomputes critical decisions on a separate path. The paper establishes the failure class and shows that several mechanisms are practical. Whether the full profile performs better than existing checks remains an open experiment.

</details>


### [25] [Can LLMs Learn and Apply Multi-Level Modelling Semantics? A First Empirical Study](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13257v1)
*Yuhong Fu,Weixing Zhang,Bowen Jiang,Haowei Cheng,Karamjti Kaur,Markus Stumptner*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 大型语言模型在多层级建模任务中表现出部分成功：语法正确性可达，但语义正确性有限，隐式约束难以捕捉，三种模型中以Claude最为均衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测试LLM能否从已有的两层建模泛化到语义更复杂的多层建模（MLM），以应对工业5.0对人机协同建模工具的需求。

Method: 使用三个商业LLM（GPT-5.4, Claude Opus 4.6, Gemini 3.1 Pro）在六种提示策略下为MULTI Warehouse Challenge生成SLICER语言的多层模型，共90个，与手动验证参考模型通过14项指标比较。

Result: 语法正确性可达；语义正确性部分实现（实例化/特化正确率52%-79%）；模型能复现显式内容但缺乏隐式约束；提示策略在精确性和完整性间权衡；自我检查仅作为规则检查器；Claude表现最均衡。

Conclusion: 当前LLM在多层建模中能力有限，这些结果为指导工业5.0中AI辅助建模工作流的设计提供了依据。

中文摘要：工业5.0强调以人为中心的工业系统设计，对建模工具提出了额外需求。多层建模（MLM）可以直接表示三个或更多抽象层次，但这以模型正确性所依赖的更复杂的语义约束为代价。大型语言模型（LLM）在模型驱动工程中的研究日益增多，但这一证据完全基于两层建模任务，而它是否能推广到语义本质上不同的MLM尚未经过测试。本文首次对这一问题进行实证研究。我们让三个商业LLM（GPT-5.4、Claude Opus 4.6和Gemini 3.1 Pro）在六种提示策略下为MULTI Warehouse Challenge生成SLICER语言的多层模型，共产生90个生成模型，并与使用十四个指标的手动验证参考模型进行比较。语法正确性在可达到范围内，但语义正确性仅部分实现，实例化/特化正确性范围从52%到79%。模型复现了任务文本中明确陈述的内容，但很少完成文本隐含但未明确说明的结构和约束。提示策略在精确性和完整性之间进行权衡，自我检查功能主要作为规则检查器，而非可靠地提高与参考设计的一致性。在三个LLM中，Claude显示出最平衡的特征。这些结果阐明了当前LLM在MLM能力上的边界，并为工业5.0中以人为中心、AI辅助的建模工作流设计提供了信息。

Original abstract: Industry 5.0 emphasises human-centric industrial system design, placing additional demands on modelling tools. Multi-level modelling (MLM) can directly represent three or more abstraction levels, but this comes at the cost of more complex semantic constraints that model correctness depends on. Large Language Models (LLMs) have been increasingly studied in model-driven engineering, but this evidence rests entirely on two-level modelling tasks, and whether it generalises to MLM, whose semantics differ in kind, remains untested. This paper presents the first empirical study of this question. We have three commercial LLMs (GPT-5.4, Claude Opus 4.6, and Gemini 3.1 Pro) generate multi-level models for the MULTI Warehouse Challenge in the SLICER language under six prompting strategies, yielding 90 generated models compared against a manually validated reference using fourteen metrics. Syntactic correctness is within reach, but semantic correctness is only partially achieved, with Instantiation/Specialisation Correctness ranging from 52% to 79%. Models reproduce content stated explicitly in the task text, but rarely complete structure and constraints the text implies without stating. Prompting strategies trade off precision against completeness, and self-checking functions mainly as a rule checker rather than reliably improving alignment with the reference design. Among the three LLMs, Claude shows the most balanced profile. These results clarify the boundaries of current LLM capability for MLM and inform the design of human-centred, AI-assisted modelling workflows for Industry 5.0.

</details>


### [26] [Faithful Autoformalization of Natural Language Assertions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13303v1)
*Hongyi Liu,Madhusudan Parthasarathy,Adithya Murali*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: Monty框架通过一致性评分和有效性测试过滤LLM生成的断言，比直接使用LLM翻译更可靠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 编写形式化合约劳动密集且易出错，LLMs虽能自动形式化但面临断言有效性和自然语言歧义挑战。

Method: 提出Monty框架，使用一致性评分和基于测试的有效性评分来过滤LLM生成的断言形式化。

Result: 在541个任务上，Monty比朴素LLM翻译在精确率上平均提升最多20个百分点。

Conclusion: Monty框架能更可靠地自动生成形式化断言，有效应对有效性和歧义问题。

中文摘要：形式化合约对于软件测试和验证至关重要，然而编写它们仍然劳动密集且容易出错。LLMs提供了一条有希望的自动形式化路径：从自然语言规范合成可执行断言，从而弥合非正式开发者意图与正式可执行规范之间的鸿沟。我们提出了Monty：一个用于断言的自动形式化框架，它应对了断言的预期有效性和自然语言中的歧义性挑战。我们的技术基于使用新颖的一致性评分度量和通过测试代码对形式化断言进行测试获得的有效性评分来过滤形式化。我们在源自22个类似集合的Java类的541个断言生成任务上评估了我们的方法，并表明我们的技术比朴素地使用LLMs翻译断言更可靠地生成ground truth（平均精确率提高最多20个百分点）。

Original abstract: Formal contracts are essential for software testing and verification, yet writing them remains labor-intensive and error-prone. LLMs offer a promising path toward autoformalization: synthesizing executable assertions from natural-language specifications and thereby bridging the gap between informal developer intent and formal executable specifications. We present Monty: an autoformalization framework for assertions that tackles the challenges of expectations of validity of assertions and ambiguity in natural-language. Our techniques are based on filtering formalizations using a novel conformance score metric and validity scores obtained from testing the code against formalized assertions. We evaluate our approach on 541 assertion-generation tasks derived from 22 collection-like Java classes, and show that our technique produces the ground truth more reliably (improving upto 20 points in precision on average) than when using LLMs naively to translate assertions.

### [27] [Natural-Language to SysMLv2 Translation via Conformance-Driven Iterative Refinement](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14162v1)
*Chance LaVoie,Eladio Andujar Lugo,Taylan G. Topcu,Levent Burak Kara*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一个基于符合性检查器驱动的框架，通过生成-检查-修复循环，将自然语言可靠翻译为SysMLv2模型，确保100%生产级接受，优于单次生成的51.16%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实际部署中，生成的SysMLv2模型必须被工业建模环境接受，而不仅仅是语法正确，现有方法缺乏对生产级符合性的保证。

Method: 构建一个包含SysMLv2符合性检查器的生成-检查-修复循环，以生产检查器作为预言机，迭代修正直到零符合性错误。

Result: 在151个提示和4个LLM后端上评估，单次生成生产符合率51.16%，本方法达到100.00%，所有模型均可加载、可视化和工程使用。

Conclusion: 将生产符合性作为生成控制机制，可将概率性LLM输出转化为可靠的生产级SysMLv2工件，提升MBSE自动化部署的可行性。

中文摘要：基于模型的系统工程（MBSE）依赖正式的系统模型作为主要技术工件，用于表示系统生命周期中的需求、结构和行为。随着SysMLv2作为文本语言的标准化，将自然语言描述直接翻译为可执行模型的兴趣日益增加。对于实际部署，生成的模型必须被工业建模环境接受，而不仅仅是满足语法约束。我们提出了一种由符合性检查器驱动的框架，用于实现从自然语言到SysMLv2的可靠翻译，该框架以生产级接受为终止条件。该系统在一个生成-检查-修复循环中嵌入了一个SysMLv2符合性检查器。每个模型都使用该检查器进行评估，并将确定性诊断纳入修订中，直到达到零符合性错误。使用生产检查器作为预言机确保了框架的目标是可部署性而非语法可行性。我们在完整的SysMBench提示集（共151个提示）上评估了该方法，使用了四个大语言模型后端，产生了604个提示-模型案例。单次生成实现了51.16%的生产符合性接受率，而我们的方法实现了100.00%的符合性。通过将生产符合性从后处理检查提升为生成过程中的控制机制，该框架将概率输出转化为生产接受的SysMLv2工件，适用于加载、可视化和工程使用。

Original abstract: Model-Based Systems Engineering (MBSE) relies on formal system models as primary technical artifacts for representing requirements, structure, and behavior across the system lifecycle. With the standardization of SysMLv2 as a textual language, interest is increasing in translating natural-language descriptions directly into executable models. For practical deployment, generated models must be accepted by industrial modeling environments, not merely satisfy grammar constraints. We present a conformance-checker-driven framework for reliable natural-language-to-SysMLv2 translation that enforces production-level acceptance as the termination condition. The system embeds a SysMLv2 conformance checker within a generate-check-repair loop. Each model is evaluated using the checker, and deterministic diagnostics are incorporated into revisions until zero conformance errors are achieved. Using the production checker as the oracle ensures the framework targets deployability rather than grammar plausibility. We evaluate the approach on the full SysMBench prompt set of 151 prompts across four large language model backends, yielding 604 prompt-model cases. Single-shot generation achieves 51.16% production-conformance acceptance, while our approach achieves 100.00% conformance. By elevating production conformance from a post-processing check to a control mechanism within generation, the framework converts probabilistic outputs into production-accepted SysMLv2 artifacts suitable for loading, visualization, and engineering use.

</details>

### [28] [Rethinking the Evaluation of Harness Evolution for Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12227v1)
*Yike Wang,Huaisheng Zhu,Zhengyu Hu,Yige Yuan,Zhengyu Chen,Shakti Senthil,Hannaneh Hajishirzi,Yulia Tsvetkov,Pradeep Dasigi,Teng Xiao*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 重新评估harness evolution方法，对agent设计有启发，可迁移至coding agent的自动优化。

TL;DR: 重新评估自动工具演化，发现其并不优于简单测试时扩展，且泛化有限，质疑现有评估协议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自动工具演化评估存在两个问题：未与简单搜索基线比较且可能过拟合，因此需要公平评估其有效性。

Method: 在相同反馈和推理预算下，比较工具演化与测试时扩展及发现基线，并在保留任务上测试泛化性。

Result: 在Terminal-Bench 2.1上，自动工具演化不持续优于简单测试时扩展，且泛化能力有限。

Conclusion: 自动工具演化的有效性存疑，需更公平的评估协议和基准。

中文摘要：我们重新审视了针对LLM智能体的自动工具演化评估。现有的工具演化方法使用单元测试用例来搜索工具配置，然后在相同的公共基准上报告最终性能。这种协议引发了两个基本问题。首先，工具演化本身是一个迭代搜索过程，它反复评估和修订候选工具，并利用任务反馈。因此，与智能体测试时扩展类似，它应该在匹配的反馈和推理预算下与简单的任务级搜索基线进行比较，以确定其收益是来自改进的工具设计还是仅仅来自额外的搜索。其次，由于搜索和最终评估共享相同的基准，报告的性能提升存在过拟合到该特定任务集的风险。为了解决这些问题，我们在可比的反馈和推理预算下，将工具演化与简单的测试时扩展和发现基线进行了广泛评估，并在保留的任务上评估演化后的工具，以判断发现的改进是否泛化。在带有GPT-5.4和Claude Opus 4.6的Terminal-Bench 2.1上的实验表明，自动工具演化并不持续优于简单的测试时扩展方法，并且表现出有限的泛化能力。我们的结果对自动工具演化的有效性提出了重要问题，并强调了更公平的评估协议和基准对于自动工具设计的必要性。我们的代码可在https://github.com/rethinking-harness-evolution获取。

Original abstract: We revisit the evaluation of automatic harness evolution for LLM agents. Existing harness evolution methods use unit test cases to search for harness configurations and then report final performance on the same public benchmark. This protocol raises two fundamental concerns. First, harness evolution is itself an iterative search procedure that repeatedly evaluates and revises candidate harnesses using task feedback. As in agentic test-time scaling, it should therefore be compared with simple task-level search baselines under matched feedback and inference budgets to determine whether its gains arise from improved harness design or from additional search alone. Second, because the search and the final evaluation share the same benchmark, the reported gains risk overfitting to that specific task set. To address these concerns, we conduct an extensive evaluation comparing harness evolution with simple test-time scaling and discovery baselines under comparable feedback and inference budgets, and also evaluate evolved harnesses on held-out tasks to assess whether the discovered improvements generalize. Experiments on Terminal-Bench 2.1 with GPT-5.4 and Claude Opus 4.6 show that automatic harness evolution does not consistently outperform simple test-time scaling methods and exhibits limited generalization. Our results raise important questions about the effectiveness of automatic harness evolution and highlight the need for fairer evaluation protocols and benchmarks for automatic harness design. Our code is available at https://github.com/rethinking-harness-evolution.

</details>


### [29] [On-Device Deep Research at 4B: Exposure Bounds Faithfulness, Retrieval Bounds Coverage](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12257v1)
*Vinay Kumar Chaganti*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究agent的信奉度和覆盖率分析，对agent设计有启示。

TL;DR: 设备端研究代理的引用忠实性受暴露量（源文本长度）驱动，而可信覆盖率受检索召回率限制；提高每源暴露量可低成本提升忠实性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测量小模型在设备端研究代理中的引用忠实性和成本，并分离影响忠实性和覆盖率的两个不同因素。

Method: 固定4B生成器在24GB笔记本上，交叉两个变量：源文本长度（400 vs 1500字符）和源质量（金标准论文 vs 检索论文），评估引用声明忠实性和可信覆盖率。

Result: 暴露量提升忠实性：检索源从0.45到0.58，金源从0.37到0.58，两者收敛；可信覆盖率在检索源上保持约0.22（因召回率约0.40）；额外暴露成本约235输出token。

Conclusion: 提高每源暴露量（低成本）是提升忠实性的有效方法；之后，检索召回率是提升覆盖率的唯一杠杆。

中文摘要：设备端研究代理在个人笔记本电脑上搜索语料库、阅读来源并撰写带引用的简报。它们的引用是否忠实，以及成本如何，对于一个可部署的小型模型来说尚未被测量。本研究固定了一个4B生成器在一台24GB的笔记本电脑上，探究什么使其引用忠实。它分离了两个通常作为一个数字报告的量。引用声明忠实性衡量被引用的来源是否支持该声明。可信覆盖率衡量代理是否也引用了正确的来源。本研究交叉了生成器看到每个源的多少（400字符对1500字符）与所提供源的质量（金标准论文对检索论文）。由此得出了两个杠杆，它们作用于不同的结果。暴露量决定了忠实性。在检索源上，更多暴露将忠实性从0.45提升到0.58，在金源上从0.37提升到0.58，且两种设置趋于收敛，因此忠实性受暴露量限制，而非源是否正确。暴露量的提升对第二个独立评判者而言是稳健的；在主要评判者下精确收敛，在第二个评判者下仅近似收敛。检索决定了覆盖率。在检索源上，可信覆盖率在任何暴露量下都保持在0.22附近，因为召回率保持在0.40附近，因此暴露量无法修复引用了哪些源。额外暴露成本约为235个输出标记。实际方案是首先廉价地提高每个源的暴露量，然后将检索召回率视为唯一的剩余杠杆。

Original abstract: On-device research agents search a corpus, read sources, and write a cited brief on a personal laptop. Whether their citations are faithful, and at what cost, is unmeasured for a deployable small model. This study fixes one 4B generator on a 24 GB laptop and asks what makes its citations faithful. It separates two quantities usually reported as one number. Cited claim faithfulness asks whether the cited source supports the claim. Trustworthy coverage asks whether the agent also cites the right sources. The study crosses how much of each source the generator sees, 400 against 1500 characters, with the quality of the sources supplied, gold papers against retrieved papers. Two levers fall out, and they act on different outcomes. Exposure sets faithfulness. More of each source lifts faithfulness from 0.45 to 0.58 on retrieved sources and from 0.37 to 0.58 on gold sources, and the two settings converge, so faithfulness is bound by exposure, not by whether the source is correct. The exposure lift is robust to a second, independent judge; the exact convergence is tight under the primary judge and only approximate under the second. Retrieval sets coverage. Trustworthy coverage stays near 0.22 on retrieved sources at any exposure, because recall is held near 0.40, so exposure cannot fix which sources are cited. The extra exposure costs about 235 output tokens. The practical recipe is to raise per source exposure first, cheaply, and then treat retrieval recall as the only remaining lever.

</details>


### [30] [How Many Tasks Are Enough for Agent Benchmark Decisions? A Replay Analysis of Public LLM Agent Benchmarks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12338v1)
*Wei-Jung Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 分析agent benchmark任务量对决策的影响，直接相关agent评测方法论。

TL;DR: 通过重放任务记录，发现部分评估所需任务比例因基准而异，报告应明确多个关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于评估成本高，常进行部分运行，但不确定部分运行能否得出与完整基准一致的结论。

Method: 重放SWE-bench、AppWorld和tau-bench的已完成任务记录，定义部分预算足够的条件并测试不同预算水平。

Result: 不同基准所需任务比例差异大：AppWorld需15%，tau-bench需25%，SWE-bench Verified需90%，SWE-bench Lite在95%时仍不满足所有目标。

Conclusion: 部分评估报告应说明性能差距、任务选择、覆盖规则、决策规则及未解决比较比例。

中文摘要：Agent基准测试通常在所有任务运行后比较两个agent，但昂贵的评估使得部分运行很诱人。仅凭任务分数并不能显示部分运行是否支持与完整基准相同的成对结论。我们通过重放来自SWE-bench、AppWorld和tau-bench的已完成公开任务级记录来研究这个问题。部分预算只有在支持完整基准的决策、覆盖所需的任务组、并且留出的未解决比较不超过目标比例时才被认为是足够的。所需的任务比例差异很大。在5个百分点预算网格上的严格0个百分点阈值下，AppWorld在15%时首次满足所有目标，tau-bench在25%，SWE-bench Verified在90%；在主要覆盖规则下，SWE-bench Lite到95%仍未满足所有目标。部分评估报告应说明一个agent必须比另一个agent高出多少、如何选择任务、需要什么样的覆盖规则、使用什么决策规则、以及可能有多少比较仍未解决。

Original abstract: Agent benchmarks often compare two agents after all tasks have run, but costly evaluations make partial runs tempting. A task fraction alone does not show whether a partial run supports the same pairwise conclusion as the completed benchmark. We study this question by replaying completed public task-level records from SWE-bench, AppWorld, and tau-bench. A partial budget counts as enough only when it supports the completed benchmark's decision, covers required task groups, and leaves no more than a target fraction of comparisons unresolved. The required task fraction varies sharply. At the strict 0 percentage point threshold on a 5 percentage point budget grid, AppWorld first meets all targets at 15 percent, tau-bench at 25 percent, and SWE-bench Verified at 90 percent; SWE-bench Lite does not meet all targets by 95 percent under the primary coverage rule. Partial-evaluation reports should state how much one agent must outperform another, how tasks are selected, what coverage rule is required, what decision rule is used, and how many comparisons may remain unresolved.

</details>


### [31] [PM-Bench: Evaluating Prospective Memory in LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.12385v1)
*Genglin Liu,Saadia Gabriel*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: PM-Bench评估agent前瞻记忆，与agent记忆能力直接相关。

TL;DR: 提出PM-Bench基准测试评估LLM agent的前瞻记忆能力，实验显示最佳模型GPT-5.4仅达65.1% F1，且无单一策略主导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Agentic AI中前瞻记忆能力不足，缺乏有效的评估基准。

Method: 受Virtual Week范式启发，设计基于文本的七天模拟环境，要求agent在持续活动中执行延迟任务。

Result: 八种LLM在八种配置下，最佳GPT-5.4仅65.1% F1，所有方法均具挑战性。

Conclusion: PM-Bench作为受控测试平台，可诊断失败并开发干预措施。

中文摘要：Agentic AI中的一个重大挑战是前瞻记忆：即在其他活动进行时，能够在特定的未来提示或状态下执行意图的能力。我们引入了PM-Bench，这是一个基于文本的基准，用于衡量现代LLM agent的前瞻记忆能力。受认知科学中Virtual Week范式的启发，PM-Bench评估LLM agent在维持用户意图、执行延迟意图以及监控潜在环境变化方面的能力。在模拟的七天一周中，agent必须继续正在进行中的活动，同时判断是否有任何延迟任务到期。我们在八种不同的agent配置下比较了八种最先进的LLM在PM-Bench上的表现。PM-Bench在所有设置下都具有挑战性：最佳方法（GPT-5.4 agent）在我们的评估中仅达到65.1%的F1分数。此外，没有一种单一的前瞻记忆改进策略能够跨模型占据主导地位。我们发布PM-Bench作为一个受控的测试平台，用于诊断这些失败并开发支持可靠前瞻行为的训练或推理时干预措施。

Original abstract: A significant challenge in agentic AI is prospective memory: the ability to execute an intention at a specific future cue or state while other activities are ongoing. We introduce PM-Bench, a text-based benchmark for measuring prospective memory capabilities in modern LLM agents. Inspired by the Virtual Week paradigm from cognitive science, PM-Bench evaluates how well LLM agents maintain user intentions, execute delayed intentions, and monitor latent environment changes. Over the course of a simulated seven-day week, agents must continue an ongoing activity while deciding whether any deferred task is due. We compare eight state-of-the-art LLMs on PM-Bench under eight different agent configurations. PM-Bench proves challenging across all settings: the best method, a GPT-5.4 agent, reaches only 65.1\% F1 score under our evaluation. Furthermore, no single strategy for improving prospective memory dominates across models. We release PM-Bench as a controlled testbed for diagnosing these failures and developing training or inference-time interventions that support reliable prospective behavior.

### [32] [ToolAnchor: Anchoring Counterfactual Context to Boost Agentic Tool-use Capability](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14145v1)
*Weiting Liu,Jieyi Bi,Wanqi Zhou,Jianfeng Feng,Yining Ma,Ai Han,Wenlian Lu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: ToolAnchor通过反事实上下文增强工具使用，通用agent方法，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: 提出ToolAnchor框架，通过反事实锚定上下文打破智能体行为惯性，实现动态工具集扩展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在工具集扩展时存在行为惯性，重新训练不现实。

Method: 使用教师模型生成反事实上下文，通过学生rollout验证，并利用智能体后训练内化成功干预。

Result: 在GAIA、BrowseComp和VDR-Bench任务上，ToolAnchor在扩展工具集下表现有竞争力。

Conclusion: 弥合了静态后训练与动态适应的差距，为可扩展的智能体强化学习开辟了新路径。

中文摘要：工具增强的大语言模型智能体在长周期任务中表现出色，但它们通常是在固定工具集上进行后训练的。当任务需要新工具时，这些智能体难以有效整合它们，而且从头重新训练往往不切实际。我们将此类工具集扩展问题的核心障碍识别为行为惯性：即尽管能够使用新工具，但智能体倾向于依赖熟悉的工具和既定的推理模式。我们证明，在关键决策点注入反事实锚定上下文可以打破这种惯性，通过唤起被抑制的智能体能力来恢复失败的轨迹。为了扩展这一见解，我们提出了ToolAnchor框架，该框架利用教师模型来假设这些反事实上下文，通过学生rollout进行验证，并通过智能体后训练内化成功的干预。在通用AI助手（GAIA）、文本搜索（BrowseComp）和视觉搜索（VDR-Bench）任务上的广泛评估表明，ToolAnchor在扩展工具集下始终表现出有竞争力的性能。我们的工作弥合了静态后训练和动态适应之间的差距，为可扩展的智能体强化学习开辟了新路径。

Original abstract: Tool-augmented large language model agents excel at long-horizon tasks, yet they are typically post-trained on fixed toolsets. When tasks demand new tools, these agents struggle to incorporate them effectively, and retraining from scratch is often impractical. We identify the core obstacle in such toolset expansion problem as behavioral inertia: the tendency of agents to fall back on familiar tools and established reasoning patterns despite having access to new ones. We demonstrate that injecting counterfactual anchor contexts at critical decision points can break this inertia, recovering failed trajectories by eliciting suppressed agent capabilities. To scale this insight, we propose ToolAnchor, a framework that uses teacher models to hypothesize these counterfactual contexts, verifies them via student rollouts, and internalizes the successful interventions through agentic post-training. Extensive evaluations across general AI assistant (GAIA), textual search (BrowseComp), and visual search (VDR-Bench) tasks demonstrate that ToolAnchor consistently exhibits competitive performance under expanded toolsets. Our work bridges the gap between static post-training and dynamic adaptation, charting a new path for scalable agentic reinforcement learning.
